CodeSystem: קוד מוצר או שירות על פי משרד הבריאות

Official URL: http://fhir.health.gov.il/cs/medical-service-moh Version: 0.13.2
Draft as of 2023-12-23 Computable Name: MedicalServiceMoH

קוד שירותים רפואיים , כולל שירותים באשפוז, שירותים אמבולטוריים, רפואת שיניים ובריאות הנפש Codes for medical services. Note that while this code system closely resembles CPT and includes a large number of CPT codes, there are some additional codes that are not covered by CPT and, more importantly, some cases where CPT codes are remapped and have different semantic meanings (e.g., code #28899 has two different meanings in CPT and in MoH codesytem). Therefore, despite apparent resemblance, this code system MUST NOT be treated as CPT.

This Code system is referenced in the content logical definition of the following value sets:

  • ILCoreProcedureCode
  • MedicalServiceMoH

This case-insensitive code system http://fhir.health.gov.il/cs/medical-service-moh defines the following codes:
